Once you have identified your bird use the app’s amazing collection of illustrations and photos to study its features and characteristics, or what birders like to call its GISS. Then use one of its 3,000 audio recordings from the famous Cornell Lab of Ornithology to invite the bird right to you! \r\n\r\niBird lets you say goodbye to large, heavy and easy-to-forget printed paper based field guides with there postage stamp sized photos and replaces them with a multimedia marvel that will teach you how bird like an expert, and provide you with literally hundreds of illustrations, photos, textual data, numeric information and song recordings and much more. iBird contains the equivalent of 14 full sized field guides and yet the app is under 600 MB.\r\n\r\nHere are just a few of the things that make iBird the perfect app for birders.\r\n\r\n▶ PATENTED INTELLIGENT \"S.A.V.E\" SEARCH ENGINE - iBird has an amazing feature called SAVE which helps you learn to ID birds like the experts. SAVE stands for Smart Attribute and Value Elimination and means that you will never be presented choices to search, which won’t lead to a result. iBird's SAVE search engine  guarantees you will never see \"no birds found.\"\r\n\r\n▶ THE WORLD’S MOST ACCLAIMED IPHONE AND ANDROID BIRDING APP now comes to Windows 8 with features that go far beyond any field guide on the planet. \r\n\r\n▶ INCLUDES 816 SPECIES OF NORTH AMERICA INCLUDING CANADA, NORTHERN MEXICO AND BAJA CALIFORNIA\r\n\r\n▶ CONTAINS HUNDREDS OF GORGEOUS HAND DRAWN ILLUSTRATIONS AND PROFESSIONAL PHOTOS – for every species. The photos are from famous nature photographers and show each species in its natural environment.\r\n\r\n▶ COMMENTS  – A FIRST – Leave messages about any bird directly on its species page, save your own notes for every species and mark the birds you have seen or like as Favorites.\r\n\r\n▶ 20 POWERFUL SEARCH ATTRIBUTES TURNS YOU INTO A MASTER BIRDER – iBird searches by location (state and provinces of Canada, coasts, oceans and seas), color, shape, size, habitat, backyard feeder, family, four kinds of color (primary, secondary, prominent, breast and crown) and much more.\r\n\r\n▶ TUTORIALS - Explain how and when to use each search attribute long with lessons on birding.\r\n\r\n▶ AUDIO SONGS AND CALLS – iBird offers 5 hours of bird songs and calls from the gold standard of recordings: the Macaulay Library at the Cornell Lab of Ornithology.  Each song or call is annotated with what it means such as alarm, territorial, attraction, etc.\r\n\r\n▶ CONFORMS TO ABA AND AOU STANDARDS –iBird follows standards set by the American Ornithological Union and the American Birding Association. As an example iBird correctly splits of the Winter Wren into the Winter and Pacific types. \r\n\r\n▶ FIRST NAME, LAST NAME OR TAXONOMIC SORT – Sort species in taxonomic (evolutionary) as well as alphabetic order.\r\n\r\nAWARDS and ACCOLADES for iBird:\r\n\r\niBird has won more awards for excellence than any birding app on the market. Containing the equivalent of 14 book-based field guides with iBird you will be able to type a few letter of any species name and see it appear instantly on the Browse screen. Don't know the name? Just enter your location, the bird's most prominent color and possibly a few other details and watch iBird's \"parametric\" decision engine find the exact bird you are looking for. It's patented algorithm makes finding a bird a simple step-by-step process where nothing can go wrong. It makes sure that the result you get is the only possible bird with those characteristics.\r\n\r\nBut iBird is a lot more than a search engine.
